See for example: https://github.com/facebookresearch/Detectron/blob/master/configs/getting_started/tutorial_1gpu_e2e_faster_rcnn_R-50-FPN.yaml#L14
When using more than one image per GPU you may encounter an out-of-memory (OOM) error if your GPU does not have sufficient memory. If this happens, you can reduce SOLVER.IMS_PER_BATCH (for training) or TEST.IMS_PER_BATCH (for inference).
